    <td>fe</td>

    <td>-</td>

    <td>.e</td>
    <td>fy,tla,stl</td>
    <td>X1= and following arguments conjoin</td>

    <td>-</td>
    <td>gu</td>
    <td></td>

  <tr>
    <td>fy</td>
    <td>S</td>
    <td>13</td>
    <td>0.1.1</td>
    <td>and</td>
    <td>-</td>
    <td>-</td>
    <td>-</td>
    <td>.e</td>
    <td>fe,tla,stl</td>
    <td>Retroactive downjump: previous argument at same level as fy goes down one level and becomes the first case of the following predicate</td>
    <td>Often used with -tla and -stl for afterthought group arguments.</td>

    <td></td>

    <td>Makes negated statement about all referent set members.  There is only one null set so it is meaningless to make statements about its members.  !xn -jy means ``nothing''.</td>
  </tr>
